*/\n\n#include <cmath>\n#include <cstdio>\n#include <cstdlib>\n#include <cstring>\n#include <vector>\n\n#include <hip/hip_bf16.h>\n#include <hip/hip_runtime.h>\n\n#ifndef KERNEL_SGB\n#define KERNEL_SGB 1\n#endif\n\n#define KD 3\n#define KH 5\n#define KW 5\n#define PaddingD 0\n#define PaddingH 2\n#define PaddingW 2\n#define BLOCK_H 45\n#define BLOCK_W 80\n#define IO_DTYPE __hip_bfloat16\n\n#if KERNEL_SGB\n#include \"kernels/conv_depthwise3d_hip_sgb.cpp\"\n#else\n#include \"kernels/conv_depthwise3d_hip.cpp\"\n#endif\n\n#define HIP_CHECK(call)                                                                            \\\n    do {                                                                                           \\\n        hipError_t err = (call);                                                                   \\\n        if (err != hipSuccess) {                                                                   \\\n            fprintf(stderr, \"%s:%d hip error: %s\\n\", __FILE__, __LINE__, hipGetErrorString(err)); \\\n            std::exit(1);                                                                          \\\n        }                                                                                          \\\n    } while (0)\n\nstatic void bf16_fill_pattern(__hip_bfloat16* dst, size_t n, unsigned seed) {\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < n; ++i) {\n        uint16_t u = static_cast<uint16_t>((seed * 1103515245u + static_cast<unsigned>(i)) & 0x7fffu);\n        u |= 0x3f00u;\n        std::memcpy(dst + i, &u, sizeof(u));\n    }\n}\n\nstatic float bf16_to_float(__hip_bfloat16 x) {\n    uint16_t bits = 0;\n    std::memcpy(&bits, &x, sizeof(bits));\n    const uint32_t u32 = static_cast<uint32_t>(bits) << 16u;\n    float f = 0.f;\n    std::memcpy(&f, &u32, sizeof(f));\n    return f;\n}\n\n// NCHW linear: in[b,c,d,h,w]\nstatic size_t lin5(int B, int C, int D, int H, int W, int b, int c, int d, int h, int w) {\n    return (((static_cast<size_t>(b) * static_cast<size_t>(C) + static_cast<size_t>(c)) * static_cast<size_t>(D) +\n             static_cast<size_t>(d)) *\n                static_cast<size_t>(H) +\n            static_cast<size_t>(h)) *\n               static_cast<size_t>(W) +\n           static_cast<size_t>(w);\n}\n\n// weight [oC, 1, KD, KH, KW] contiguous like PyTorch (in_channels/groups == 1)\nstatic size_t lin_w(int oC, int kd, int kh, int kw) {\n    const size_t per_oc = static_cast<size_t>(KD) * KH * KW;\n    return static_cast<size_t>(oC) * per_oc + static_cast<size_t>(kd) * static_cast<size_t>(KH * KW) +\n           static_cast<size_t>(kh) * static_cast<size_t>(KW) + static_cast<size_t>(kw);\n}\n\n/*\n * CPU reference: depthwise conv3d, stride=1, dilation=1, same padding as kernel.\n * Matches torch.nn.functional.conv3d with groups=C (depthwise).\n */\nstatic void cpu_depthwise_conv3d_ref(const std::vector<__hip_bfloat16>& in_bf16,\n                                     const std::vector<__hip_bfloat16>& w_bf16,\n                                     const std::vector<__hip_bfloat16>& bias_bf16, std::vector<float>& out_f32, int B,\n                                     int C, int D, int H, int W, int C_out, int D_out, int H_out, int W_out) {\n    out_f32.assign(static_cast<size_t>(B) * C_out * D_out * H_out * W_out, 0.f);\n    const int stride_d = 1, stride_h = 1, stride_w = 1;\n    const int dil_d = 1, dil_h = 1, dil_w = 1;\n\n    for (int b = 0; b < B; ++b) {\n        for (int oc = 0; oc < C_out; ++oc) {\n            const int ic = oc;\n            const float bias = bf16_to_float(bias_bf16[static_cast<size_t>(oc)]);\n            for (int od = 0; od < D_out; ++od) {\n                for (int oh = 0; oh < H_out; ++oh) {\n                    for (int ow = 0; ow < W_out; ++ow) {\n                        float acc = bias;\n                        for (int kd = 0; kd < KD; ++kd) {\n                            for (int kh = 0; kh < KH; ++kh) {\n                                for (int kw = 0; kw < KW; ++kw) {\n                                    const int id = od * stride_d - PaddingD + kd * dil_d;\n                                    const int ih = oh * stride_h - PaddingH + kh * dil_h;\n                                    const int iw = ow * stride_w - PaddingW + kw * dil_w;\n                                    if (id < 0 || id >= D || ih < 0 || ih >= H || iw < 0 || iw >= W) {\n                                        continue;\n                                    }\n                                    const float iv =\n                                        bf16_to_float(in_bf16[lin5(B, C, D, H, W, b, ic, id, ih, iw)]);\n                                    const float wv = bf16_to_float(w_bf16[lin_w(oc, kd, kh, kw)]);\n                                    acc += iv * wv;\n                                }\n                            }\n                        }\n                        out_f32[lin5(B, C_out, D_out, H_out, W_out, b, oc, od, oh, ow)] = acc;\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nstatic void print_bytes_line(const char* label, size_t bytes) {\n    const double mib = static_cast<double>(bytes) / (1024.0 * 1024.0);\n    printf(\"  %-14s %10zu B  (%8.2f MiB)\\n\", label, bytes, mib);\n}\n\nstatic void print_run_header(int device_id) {\n    hipDeviceProp_t prop{};\n    HIP_CHECK(hipGetDeviceProperties(&prop, device_id));\n    printf(\"\\n\");\n    printf(\"=== Depthwise Conv3D BF16 (%s) ===\\n\", KERNEL_SGB ? \"sgb (sched_group_barrier variant)\" : void print_problem_and_memory(int B, int C, int D, int H, int W, int C_out, int D_out, int H_out, int W_out,\n                                     size_t n_in, size_t n_out, size_t n_w, size_t n_bias) {\n    const size_t bsz = sizeof(__hip_bfloat16);\n    const size_t bytes_in = n_in * bsz;\n    const size_t bytes_out = n_out * bsz;\n    const size_t bytes_w = n_w * bsz;\n    const size_t bytes_bias = n_bias * bsz;\n    const size_t bytes_dev = bytes_in + bytes_out + bytes_w + bytes_bias;\n\n    printf(\"\\n--- Problem (case3-style depthwise) ---\\n\");\n    printf(\"  Input NCHW:   [%d, %d, %d, %d, %d]  BF16\\n\", B, C, D, H, W);\n    printf(\"  Weight:       [%d, 1, %d, %d, %d]  BF16  (groups=%d depthwise)\\n\", C_out, KD, KH, KW, C);\n    printf(\"  Output NCHW:  [%d, %d, %d, %d, %d]  BF16\\n\", B, C_out, D_out, H_out, W_out);\n    printf(\"  stride=(1,1,1)  dilation=(1,1,1)  padding=(%d,%d,%d)\\n\", PaddingD, PaddingH, PaddingW);\n\n    printf(\"\\n--- Device buffers ---\\n\");\n    print_bytes_line(\"input\", bytes_in);\n    print_bytes_line(\"output\", bytes_out);\n    print_bytes_line(\"weights\", bytes_w);\n    print_bytes_line(\"bias\", bytes_bias);\n    print_bytes_line(\"total alloc\", bytes_dev);\n}\n\nstatic void print_kernel_config(dim3 grid, dim3 block) {\n    const long long total_blocks = static_cast<long long>(grid.x) * grid.y * grid.z;\n    const int threads_per_block = block.x * block.y * block.z;\n    const long long total_threads = total_blocks * threads_per_block;\n\n    printf(\"\\n--- Kernel configuration ---\\n\");\n    printf(\"  Kernel symbol: conv_depthwise3d_hip   (__launch_bounds__(256, 1) in HIP source)\\n\");\n    printf(\"  Compile-time: KD=%d KH=%d KW=%d  PaddingD/H/W=%d/%d/%d  BLOCK_H=%d BLOCK_W=%d  IO_DTYPE=BF16\\n\", KD, KH,\n           KW, PaddingD, PaddingH, PaddingW, BLOCK_H, BLOCK_W);\n    printf(\"  Block:  (%d, %d, %d) -> %d threads / block\\n\", block.x, block.y, block.z, const double gbps = bytes_hbm / sec / 1e9;\n\n    printf(\"\\n--- Performance (same style as gemm samples) ---\\n\");\n    printf(\"  niter (timed):        %d\\n\", niter);\n    printf(\"  Average tflops);\n    printf(\"  Efficive Bandwidth:   %.1f GB/s \\n\", gbps);\n}\n\nstatic bool check_output_bf16_vs_ref(const std::vector<__hip_bfloat16>& gpu_out,\n                                     const std::vector<float>& ref_f32, float atol, float rtol, int B, int C_out,\n                                     int D_out, int H_out, int W_out) {\n    size_t bad = 0;\n    float max_abs = 0.f;\n    size_t first_i = 0;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < ref_f32.size(); ++i) {\n        const float g = bf16_to_float(gpu_out[i]);\n        const float r = ref_f32[i];\n        const float diff = std::fabs(g - r);\n        const float tol = atol + rtol * std::fabs(r);\n        if (diff > tol) {\n            if (bad == 0) {\n                first_i = i;\n            }\n            ++bad;\n            max_abs = std::fmax(max_abs, diff);\n        }\n    }\n    if (bad > 0) {\n        fprintf(stderr,\n                \"\\n=== Correctness ===\\n\"\n                \"FAIL: %zu / %zu elements outside tol (atol=%g rtol=%g)\\n\"\n                \"  max_abs_err=%g  first_idx=%zu  gpu=%g  ref=%g\\n\",\n                bad, ref_f32.size(), atol, rtol, max_abs, first_i, bf16_to_float(gpu_out[first_i]),\n                ref_f32[first_i]);\n        return false;\n    }\n    printf(\"\\n=== Correctness ===\\n\");\n    printf(\"PASS: all %zu outputs within atol=%g rtol=%g (CPU float32 reference, zero pad like conv3d)\\n\",\n           ref_f32.size(), atol, rtol);\n    return true;\n}\n\nint main(int argc, char** argv) {\n    int niter = 10;\n    int warmup = Weights are read from s_weight via\n    // ds_read_b32 broadcast loads in 5-float chunks (one row at a time),\n    // so we never hold more than ~5 weight vregs at once.\n    for (int oi = KW_PACK*threadIdx.x; oi < num_outputs; oi += KW_PACK*blockDim.x) {\n        const int oh = oi / BLOCK_W;\n        const int ow = oi % BLOCK_W;\n        const int srci0 = oh * padded_W + ow;\n\n        IO_DTYPE d_input[KH][KWR][KW_PACK];\n\n        float sum0 = bias_value;\n        float sum1 = bias_value;\n\n        #pragma unroll\n        for(int d = 0; d < KD; d++) {\n            // Issue ds_read for this d-slice only (15 dwords).\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int h = 0; h < KH; h++) {\n                #pragma unroll\n                for(int w = 0; w < KW; w += KW_PACK) {\n                    int src_off = d*(padded_H * padded_W) + (PaddingH + h - KH/2)*padded_W + (PaddingW + w - KW/2);\n                    reinterpret_cast<uint32_t&>(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK]) = ds_read_b32(s_input + srci0, src_off*sizeof(IO_DTYPE));\n                }\n            }\n            s_waitcnt_lgkmcnt<0>();\n            __builtin_amdgcn_sched_barrier(0);\n\n            // MACs for this d-slice.  Weights for the current (d,h) row are\n            // broadcast-loaded from s_weight into 5 float vregs, then reused\n            // across the 5 p=0 / 5 p=1 MACs for that row before being\n            // discarded.\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int h = 0; h < KH; h++) {\n                const int wbase = (d * KH + h) * KW;\n                float w0 = __ldg(reinterpret_cast<const float*>(&s_weight[wbase + 0]));\n                float w1 = __ldg(reinterpret_cast<const float*>(&s_weight[wbase + 1]));\n                float w2 = __ldg(reinterpret_cast<const float*>(&s_weight[wbase + 2]));\n                float w3 = __ldg(reinterpret_cast<const float*>(&s_weight[wbase + 3]));\n                float w4 = __ldg(reinterpret_cast<const float*>(&s_weight[wbase + 4]));\n\n                // p=0 (output column ow+0)\n                v_fmac_f32(sum0, w0, (float)(d_input[h][0][0]));\n                v_fmac_f32(sum0, w1, (float)(d_input[h][0][1]));\n                v_fmac_f32(sum0, w2, (float)(d_input[h][1][0]));\n                v_fmac_f32(sum0, w3, (float)(d_input[h][1][1]));\n                v_fmac_f32(sum0, w4, (float)(d_input[h][2][0]));\n\n                // p=1 (output column ow+1)\n                v_fmac_f32(sum1, w0, (float)(d_input[h][0][1]));\n                v_fmac_f32(sum1, w1, (float)(d_input[h][1][0]));\n                v_fmac_f32(sum1, w2, (float)(d_input[h][1][1]));\n                v_fmac_f32(sum1, w3, (float)(d_input[h][2][0]));\n                v_fmac_f32(sum1, w4, (float)(d_input[h][2][1]));\n            }\n        }\n\n        output[oh * oW + ow + 0] = (IO_DTYPE)(sum0);\n        output[oh * oW + ow + 1] = (IO_DTYPE)(sum1);\n    }\n}\nKERNEL_EOF\ncp /app/kernels/conv_depthwise3d_hip.cpp /app/kernels/conv_depthwise3d_hip_sgb.cpp\nHIP_ARCH=gfx950 ./build.sh 2>&1 | tail -3\n./conv3d_depthwise_original 5 2 2>&1 | tail -10","time":{"start":1784470648807,"end":1784470648811}},"id":"prt_f7abd1eb4001zKYj8pu7TwJF87","sessionID":"ses_08552e1eaffeJdbrpgR8hJ8F4e","messageID":"msg_f7abc1300001FhAgdrRnZJVt3C"}}

}\n\nconstexpr int LDS_SIZE = 32*1024;       // with 64-KB LDS, this allows occupancy=2\nconstexpr int weight_size = KD*KH*KW;   // in unit of IO_DTYPE\nconstexpr int max_input_size = LDS_SIZE/sizeof(IO_DTYPE) - (weight_size + 31)/32 * 32;\n\nstatic_assert(PaddingD == 0);\nusing int32x4_t = __attribute__((__vector_size__(4 * sizeof(int)))) int;\nusing as3_uint32_ptr = __attribute__((address_space(3))) uint32_t *;\n\ntemplate<uint16_t cnt>\n__device__ __inline__ void s_waitcnt_lgkmcnt() { asm volatile (\"s_waitcnt lgkmcnt(%0)\\n\"::\"i\"(cnt)); }\ntemplate<uint16_t cnt>\n__device__ __inline__ void s_waitcnt_vmcnt() { asm volatile (\"s_waitcnt vmcnt(%0)\\n\"::\"i\"(cnt)); }\n\n__device__ __inline__ uint32_t ds_read_b32(IO_DTYPE* psrc, int imm_offset=0) {\n    uint32_t v;\n    as3_uint32_ptr vaddr = (as3_uint32_ptr)(psrc);\n    asm volatile(\"ds_read_b32 %[vdst], %[vaddr] offset:%[offset]\"\n                : [vdst]\"=v\"((uint32_t&)(v))\n                : [vaddr]\"v\"(vaddr),[offset]\"i\"(imm_offset)\n                : \"memory\");\n    return v;\n}\n\n__device__ __inline__ void v_fmac_f32(float& vdst, float src0, float vsrc1) {\n    asm volatile(\"v_fmac_f32 %[vdst], %[src0], %[vsrc1]\"\n                : [vdst]\"+v\"(vdst)\n                : [src0]\"v\"(src0),[vsrc1]\"v\"(vsrc1));\n}\n\n__device__ __inline__ void set_m0(void* base) {\n    as3_uint32_ptr lds_offset = (as3_uint32_ptr)(base);\n    asm volatile(\"s_mov_b32 m0, %0\\n\\ts_nop 1\\n\\ts_nop 1\\n\"::\"s\"(lds_offset));\n}\n\n__device__ __inline__ void global_load_lds_dword(int vaddr, const void* saddr, int imm_offset = 0) {\n    asm volatile(\"global_load_lds_dword %[vaddr], %[saddr] offset:%[offset]\"\n                :: [vaddr]\"v\"(vaddr), [saddr]\"s\"(saddr), [offset]\"i\"(imm_offset)\n                : \"memory\");\n}\n\n__global__ void __launch_bounds__(256, 1) conv_depthwise3d_hip(\n    const IO_DTYPE* __restrict__ input,\n    IO_DTYPE* __restrict__ output,\n    const IO_DTYPE* __restrict__ kernel,\n    const IO_DTYPE* __restrict__ bias,\n    int iC, int iD, int iH, int iW, int oC, int oD, int oH, int oW)\n{\n    const int channel_multiplier = oC / iC;\n    const int batch = blockIdx.x;\n    const int out_channel = blockIdx.y;\n    const int out_D = blockIdx.z;\n    const int in_channel = out_channel / channel_multiplier;\n    int blk_in = (batch * iC + in_channel) * iD + out_D;\n    int blk_out = (batch * oC + out_channel) * oD + out_D;\n\n    // Weights cached in vregs (75 floats).  This is the \"function-scope\"\n    // weight_reg used by the original kernel; we keep it because it lets us\n    // avoid the per-MAC global memory round-trips.\n    float weight_reg[KD][KH][KW];\n    __shared__ IO_DTYPE s_input[max_input_size];\n\n    kernel += out_channel * weight_size;\n    input += blk_in * iH * iW;\n    output += blk_out * oH * oW;\n\n    constexpr int padded_H = PaddingH*2 + BLOCK_H;\n    constexpr int padded_W = PaddingW*2 + BLOCK_W;\n    constexpr int input_size_dw4 = (KD * padded_H * padded_W * sizeof(IO_DTYPE) + sizeof(int32x4_t) - 1)/sizeof(int32x4_t);\n    constexpr int32x4_t vzero = {0};\n    for (int i = threadIdx.x; d < KD; d++) {\n        for (int h = warp_id; h < BLOCK_H; h += num_warps) {\n            const int off_h0 = d * iH * iW + h * iW;\n            const int off_h1 = d * padded_H * padded_W + (h + PaddingH) * padded_W + PaddingW;\n            #pragma unroll\n            for (int w = lane_id; w < BLOCK_W/2; w += warp_size) {\n                set_m0(s_input + off_h1 + 2*__builtin_amdgcn_readfirstlane(w));\n                global_load_lds_dword(off_h0 * sizeof(IO_DTYPE) + w*sizeof_dword, input);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    int ki = 0;\n    #pragma unroll\n    for(int d = 0; d < KD; d ++) {\n        #pragma unroll\n        for(int h = 0; h < KH; h++) {\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int w = 0; w < KW; w++) {\n                weight_reg[d][h][w] = kernel[ki++];\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    float bias_value = 0.0f;\n    if (bias != nullptr)\n        bias_value = bias[out_channel];\n\n    s_waitcnt_vmcnt<0>();\n    __syncthreads();\n\n    constexpr int num_outputs = BLOCK_H * BLOCK_W;\n    constexpr int KW_PACK = 2;\n    constexpr int KWR = div_up(KW, KW_PACK);\n    static_assert(BLOCK_W % 2 == 0);\n\n    // Hot loop.  Two changes from the original:\n    //\n    //  (1) \"load everything then compute everything\" is replaced by a\n    //      per-d-slice schedule: for each of the 3 d-slices we issue the\n    //      15 ds_reads that bring the slice's BF16 inputs into registers,\n    //      s_waitcnt_lgkmcnt<0>, and then run the 25 v_fmac MACs that\n    //      consume them.  Because the 15 dword d_input[] array is reused\n    //      across the 3 d iterations, the per-thread input register\n    //      footprint drops from KD*KH*KWR=45 dwords to KH*KWR=15 dwords.\n    //\n    //  (2) The p=0 / p=1 outer loops are fused: instead of doing a full\n    //      pass over the kernel for output column ow, then a full pass\n    //      for column ow+1, both accumulators advance together inside a\n    //      single (d, h, w) loop.  This shares the input and weight\n    //      register reads across the two output columns.\n    for (int oi = KW_PACK*threadIdx.x; oi < num_outputs; oi += KW_PACK*blockDim.x) {\n        const int oh = oi / BLOCK_W;\n        const int ow = oi % BLOCK_W;\n        const int srci0 = oh * padded_W + ow;\n\n        IO_DTYPE d_input[KH][KWR][KW_PACK];\n\n        float sum0 = bias_value;\n        float sum1 = bias_value;\n\n        #pragma unroll\n        for(int d = 0; d < KD; d++) {\n            // Issue ds_read for this d-slice only (15 dwords).\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int h = 0; h < KH; h++) {\n                #pragma unroll\n                for(int w = 0; w < KW; w += KW_PACK) {\n                    int src_off = d*(padded_H * padded_W) + (PaddingH + h - KH/2)*padded_W + (PaddingW + w - KW/2);\n                    reinterpret_cast<uint32_t&>(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK]) = ds_read_b32(s_input + srci0, src_off*sizeof(IO_DTYPE));\n                }\n            }\n            s_waitcnt_lgkmcnt<0>();\n            __builtin_amdgcn_sched_barrier(0);\n\n            // MACs for this d-slice.  Combined p=0 / p=1 fused into single loop.\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int h = 0; h < KH; h++) {\n                #pragma unroll\n                for(int w = 0; w < KW; w += KW_PACK) {\n                    v_fmac_f32(sum0, weight_reg[d][h][w+0], (float)(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK][0]));\n                    if (w+1 < KW)\n                        v_fmac_f32(sum0, weight_reg[d][h][w+1], (float)(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK][1]));\n                    v_fmac_f32(sum1, weight_reg[d][h][w+0], (float)(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK][1]));\n                    if (w+1 < KW)\n                        v_fmac_f32(sum1, weight_reg[d][h][w+1], (float)(d_input[h][(w+KW_PACK)/KW_PACK][0]));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        output[oh * oW + ow + 0] = (IO_DTYPE)(sum0);\n        output[oh * oW + ow + 1] = (IO_DTYPE)(sum1);\n    }\n}\nKERNEL_EOF\ncp /app/kernels/conv_depthwise3d_hip.cpp /app/kernels/conv_depthwise3d_hip_sgb.cpp\nHIP_ARCH=gfx950 ./build.sh 2>&1 | tail -3\necho \"=== v1 (interleaved, weights in regs) ===\"\nfor i in 1 2 3; }\ntemplate<uint16_t cnt>\n__device__ __inline__ void s_waitcnt_vmcnt() { asm volatile (\"s_waitcnt vmcnt(%0)\\n\"::\"i\"(cnt)); }\n\n__device__ __inline__ uint32_t ds_read_b32(IO_DTYPE* psrc, int imm_offset=0) {\n    uint32_t v;\n    as3_uint32_ptr vaddr = (as3_uint32_ptr)(psrc);\n    asm volatile(\"ds_read_b32 %[vdst], %[vaddr] offset:%[offset]\"\n                : [vdst]\"=v\"((uint32_t&)(v))\n                : [vaddr]\"v\"(vaddr),[offset]\"i\"(imm_offset)\n                : \"memory\");\n    return v;\n}\n\n__device__ __inline__ void v_fmac_f32(float& vdst, float src0, float vsrc1) {\n    asm volatile(\"v_fmac_f32 %[vdst], %[src0], %[vsrc1]\"\n                : [vdst]\"+v\"(vdst)\n                : [src0]\"v\"(src0),[vsrc1]\"v\"(vsrc1));\n}\n\n__device__ __inline__ void set_m0(void* base) {\n    as3_uint32_ptr lds_offset = (as3_uint32_ptr)(base);\n    asm volatile(\"s_mov_b32 m0, %0\\n\\ts_nop 1\\n\\ts_nop 1\\n\"::\"s\"(lds_offset));\n}\n\n__device__ __inline__ void global_load_lds_dword(int vaddr, const void* saddr, int imm_offset = 0) {\n    asm volatile(\"global_load_lds_dword %[vaddr], %[saddr] offset:%[offset]\"\n                :: [vaddr]\"v\"(vaddr), [saddr]\"s\"(saddr), [offset]\"i\"(imm_offset)\n                : \"memory\");\n}\n\n__global__ void __launch_bounds__(256, 1) conv_depthwise3d_hip(\n    const IO_DTYPE* __restrict__ input,\n    IO_DTYPE* __restrict__ output,\n    const IO_DTYPE* __restrict__ kernel,\n    const IO_DTYPE* __restrict__ bias,\n    int iC, int iD, int iH, int iW, int oC, int oD, int oH, int oW)\n{\n    const int channel_multiplier = oC / iC;\n    const int batch = blockIdx.x;\n    const int out_channel = blockIdx.y;\n    const int out_D = blockIdx.z;\n    const int in_channel = out_channel / channel_multiplier;\n    int blk_in = (batch * iC + in_channel) * iD + out_D;\n    int blk_out = (batch * oC + out_channel) * oD + out_D;\n\n    // Weights cached in vregs (75 floats).  This is the \"function-scope\"\n    // weight_reg used by the original kernel; we keep it because it lets us\n    // avoid the per-MAC global memory round-trips.\n    float weight_reg[KD][KH][KW];\n    __shared__ IO_DTYPE s_input[max_input_size];\n\n    kernel += out_channel * weight_size;\n    input += blk_in * iH * iW;\n    output += blk_out * oH * oW;\n\n    constexpr int padded_H = PaddingH*2 + BLOCK_H;\n    constexpr int padded_W = PaddingW*2 + BLOCK_W;\n    constexpr int input_size_dw4 = (KD * padded_H * padded_W * sizeof(IO_DTYPE) + sizeof(int32x4_t) - 1)/sizeof(int32x4_t);\n    constexpr int32x4_t vzero = {0};\n    for (int i = threadIdx.x; i < KD * padded_H * padded_W; i += blockDim.x) {\n        s_input[i] = 0.0f;\n    }\n    __syncthreads();\n\n    constexpr int num_warps = 4;\n    constexpr int warp_size = 64;\n    constexpr int sizeof_dword = 4;\n    const int warp_id = __builtin_amdgcn_readfirstlane(threadIdx.x >> 6);\n    const int lane_id = threadIdx.x & (warp_size - 1);\n\n    // load input\n    for (int d = 0; d < KD; d++) {\n        for (int h = warp_id; h < BLOCK_H; h += num_warps) {\n            const int off_h0 = d * iH * iW + h * iW;\n            const int off_h1 = d * padded_H * padded_W + (h + PaddingH) * padded_W + PaddingW;\n            #pragma unroll\n            for (int w = lane_id; w < BLOCK_W/2; w += warp_size) {\n                set_m0(s_input + off_h1 + 2*__builtin_amdgcn_readfirstlane(w));\n                global_load_lds_dword(off_h0 * sizeof(IO_DTYPE) + w*sizeof_dword, input);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    int ki = 0;\n    #pragma unroll\n    for(int d = 0; d < KD; d ++) {\n        #pragma unroll\n        for(int h = 0; h < KH; h++) {\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int w = 0; w < KW; w++) {\n                weight_reg[d][h][w] = kernel[ki++];\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    float bias_value = 0.0f;\n    if (bias != nullptr)\n        bias_value = bias[out_channel];\n\n    s_waitcnt_vmcnt<0>();\n    __syncthreads();\n\n    constexpr int num_outputs = BLOCK_H * BLOCK_W;\n    constexpr int KW_PACK = 2;\n    constexpr int KWR = div_up(KW, KW_PACK);\n    static_assert(BLOCK_W % 2 == 0);\n\n    // Hot loop.  Two changes from the original:\n    //\n    //  (1) \"load everything then compute everything\" is replaced by a\n    //      per-d-slice schedule: for each of the 3 d-slices we issue the\n    //      15 ds_reads that bring the slice's BF16 inputs into registers,\n    //      s_waitcnt_lgkmcnt<0>, and then run the 25 v_fmac MACs that\n    //      consume them.  Because the 15 dword d_input[] array is reused\n    //      across the 3 d iterations, the per-thread input register\n    //      footprint drops from KD*KH*KWR=45 dwords to KH*KWR=15 dwords.\n    //\n    //  (2) The p=0 / p=1 outer loops are fused: instead of doing a full\n    //      pass over the kernel for output column ow, then a full pass\n    //      for column ow+1, both accumulators advance together inside a\n    //      single (d, h, w) loop.  This shares the input and weight\n    //      register reads across the two output columns.\n    for (int oi = KW_PACK*threadIdx.x; oi < num_outputs; oi += KW_PACK*blockDim.x) {\n        const int oh = oi / BLOCK_W;\n        const int ow = oi % BLOCK_W;\n        const int srci0 = oh * padded_W + ow;\n\n        IO_DTYPE d_input[KH][KWR][KW_PACK];\n\n        float sum0 = bias_value;\n        float sum1 = bias_value;\n\n        #pragma unroll\n        for(int d = 0; d < KD; d++) {\n            // Issue ds_read for this d-slice only (15 dwords).\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int h = 0; h < KH; h++) {\n                #pragma unroll\n                for(int w = 0; w < KW; w += KW_PACK) {\n                    int src_off = d*(padded_H * padded_W) + (PaddingH + h - KH/2)*padded_W + (PaddingW + w - KW/2);\n                    reinterpret_cast<uint32_t&>(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK]) = ds_read_b32(s_input + srci0, src_off*sizeof(IO_DTYPE));\n                }\n            }\n            s_waitcnt_lgkmcnt<0>();\n            __builtin_amdgcn_sched_barrier(0);\n\n            // MACs for this d-slice.  Combined p=0 / p=1 fused into single loop.\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int h = 0; h < KH; h++) {\n                #pragma unroll\n                for(int w = 0; w < KW; w += KW_PACK) {\n                    v_fmac_f32(sum0, weight_reg[d][h][w+0], (float)(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK][0]));\n                    if (w+1 < KW)\n                        v_fmac_f32(sum0, weight_reg[d][h][w+1], (float)(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK][1]));\n                    v_fmac_f32(sum1, weight_reg[d][h][w+0], (float)(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK][1]));\n                    if (w+1 < KW)\n                        v_fmac_f32(sum1, weight_reg[d][h][w+1], (float)(d_input[h][(w+KW_PACK)/KW_PACK][0]));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        output[oh * oW + ow + 0] = (IO_DTYPE)(sum0);\n        output[oh * oW + ow + 1] = (IO_DTYPE)(sum1);\n    }\n}\nKERNEL_EOF\ncp /app/kernels/conv_depthwise3d_hip.cpp /app/kernels/conv_depthwise3d_hip_sgb.cpp\nHIP_ARCH=gfx950 ./build.sh 2>&1 | tail -3\necho \"=== v1 (interleaved, weights in regs) ===\"\nfor i in 1 2 3; do\n  ./conv3d_depthwise_original 100 20 2>&1 | grep \"Throughput\"\ndone\necho \"\"\nhipcc -std=c++17 -O3 -g --offload-arch=gfx950 -DKERNEL_SGB=0 -S /app/bench_conv3d.cpp -o /tmp/opencode/isa/bench_v1.s 2>&1 | tail -3\ngrep \"vgpr_count\" /tmp/opencode/isa/bench_v1.s","time":{"start":1784470833906,"end":1784470833909}},"id":"prt_f7abfc2ff001Lqbg3mP969bm6d","sessionID":"ses_08552e1eaffeJdbrpgR8hJ8F4e","messageID":"msg_f7abeb362001v7W9xJQo3PkCTe"}}

IO_DTYPE* __restrict__ output,\n    const IO_DTYPE* __restrict__ kernel,\n    const IO_DTYPE* __restrict__ bias,\n    int iC, int iD, int iH, int iW, int oC, int oD, int oH, int oW)\n{\n    const int channel_multiplier;\n    int blk_in = (batch * iC + in_channel) * iD + out_D;\n    int blk_out = (batch * oC + out_channel) * oD + out_D;\n\n    // Weights cached in vregs (75 floats). i < KD * padded_H * padded_W; i += blockDim.x) {\n        s_input[i] = 0.0f;\n    }\n    __syncthreads();\n\n    constexpr int num_warps = 4;\n    constexpr int warp_size = 64;\n    constexpr int sizeof_dword = 4;\n    const int warp_id = __builtin_amdgcn_readfirstlane(threadIdx.x >> 6);\n    const int lane_id = threadIdx.x & (warp_size - 1);\n\n    // load input\n    for (int d = 0; This shares the input and weight\n    //      register reads across the two output columns.\n    for (int oi = KW_PACK*threadIdx.x; oi < num_outputs; oi += KW_PACK*blockDim.x) {\n        const int oh = oi / BLOCK_W;\n        const int ow = oi % BLOCK_W;\n        const int srci0 = oh * padded_W + ow;\n\n        IO_DTYPE d_input[KH][KWR][KW_PACK];\n\n        float sum0 = bias_value;\n        float sum1 = bias_value;\n\n        #pragma unroll\n        for(int d = 0; d < KD; d++) {\n            // Issue ds_read for this d-slice only (15 dwords).\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int h = 0; h < KH; h++) {\n                #pragma unroll\n                for(int w = 0; w < KW; w += KW_PACK) {\n                    int src_off = d*(padded_H * padded_W) + (PaddingH + h - KH/2)*padded_W + (PaddingW + w - KW/2);\n                    reinterpret_cast<uint32_t&>(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK]) = ds_read_b32(s_input + srci0, src_off*sizeof(IO_DTYPE));\n                }\n            }\n            s_waitcnt_lgkmcnt<0>();\n            __builtin_amdgcn_sched_barrier(0);\n\n            // MACs for this d-slice.  Combined p=0 / p=1 fused into single loop.\n            #pragma unroll\n            for(int h = 0; h < KH; h++) {\n                #pragma unroll\n                for(int w = 0; w < KW; w += KW_PACK) {\n                    v_fmac_f32(sum0, weight_reg[d][h][w+0], (float)(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK][0]));\n                    if (w+1 < KW)\n                        v_fmac_f32(sum0, weight_reg[d][h][w+1], (float)(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK][1]));\n                    v_fmac_f32(sum1, weight_reg[d][h][w+0], (float)(d_input[h][w/KW_PACK][1]));\n                    if (w+1 < KW)\n                        v_fmac_f32(sum1, weight_reg[d][h][w+1], (float)(d_input[h][(w+KW_PACK)/KW_PACK][0]));\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        output[oh * oW + ow + 0] = (IO_DTYPE)(sum0);\n        output[oh * oW + ow + 1] = (IO_DTYPE)(sum1);\n    }\n}","lineStart":1,"lineEnd":202,"totalLines":202,"truncated":false}},"title":"app/kernels/conv_depthwise3d_hip.cpp","time":{"start":1784470953564,"end":1784470953568}},"id":"prt_f7ac1de580010Kt9qIsmj7Mwmz","sessionID":"ses_08552e1eaffeJdbrpgR8hJ8F4e","messageID":"msg_f7ac1d38c001rVmZqH1Zbftbf1"}}
